## Review Protocol

1. Open the primary source candidate first and verify year, title, authors, venue, and core contribution.
2. Manually review only claims marked `needs-manual-source-review`, prioritizing absolute, first/only, proof/solved, superlative, and strong legacy wording.
3. Low-priority risk claims do not need rewriting unless a reviewer spots an unsupported source chain.
4. Re-run `npm run generate && npm run audit:ai100-accuracy` after edits.

| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Newell and Simon's 1956 paper described a system for discovering proofs in symbolic logic. | structural-only |

| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 纽厄尔和西蒙 1956 年论文描述了一个能在符号逻辑中发现证明的系统。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 谷歌图书保存了书目信息和摘要，卡内基梅隆大学档案记录了 1956 年修订版。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The display idea is proof search: start with a goal theorem, try symbolic transformations, and use heuristics to avoid blind enumeration. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | This makes reasoning visible as a sequence of choices. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 展示重点是证明搜索：从目标定理出发，尝试符号变换，并用启发式规则避免盲目穷举。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 这让推理成为一串可见的选择过程。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | proof/solved wording | Experts generally treat Logic Theorist as a founding symbolic AI system and an early proof that heuristic search could model reasoning. | needs-manual-source-review |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the combination of theorem proving, symbolic programming, cognitive modeling, and search as a practical AI pattern. | structural-only |

### milestone-1965-resolution-method - Resolution Method

Sources:
- [A Machine-Oriented Logic Based on the Resolution Principle](https://doi.org/10.1145/321250.321253) (Paper primary-candidate)
- [Journal of Symbolic Logic review record](https://www.cambridge.org/core/journals/journal-of-symbolic-logic/article/j-a-robinson-a-machineoriented-logic-based-on-the-resolution-principle-journal-of-the-association-for-computing-machinery-vol-12-1965-pp-2341/65679C30B9D7D7763FFB700CA77B18B1) (Review primary-candidate)
- [Stanford Encyclopedia: Automated Reasoning](https://plato.stanford.edu/entries/reasoning-automated/) (Background)

| Field | Locale | Risk | Manual Review | Claim | Status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| year-title | en | no | no | 1965: Resolution Method | structural-only |
| year-title | zh | no | no | 1965: 归结方法 | structural-only |
| location | en | no | no | Argonne National Laboratory / Syracuse University, Illinois and New York, United States | structural-only |
| location | zh | no | no | 阿贡国家实验室 / 雪城大学，美国伊利诺伊州与纽约州 | structural-only |
| figure | en | no | no | John Alan Robinson - Inventor of the resolution principle | structural-only |
| figure | zh | no | no | 约翰·艾伦·罗宾逊 - 归结原理提出者 | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Resolution turned first-order theorem proving into a uniform refutation procedure: translate statements into clauses, negate the target, and derive a contradiction. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Robinson combined resolution with unification, giving automated provers a compact rule that could be implemented systematically. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | It became a foundation for logic programming, SAT/SMT lineage, and many later reasoning systems. | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 归结方法把一阶定理证明变成统一的反驳过程：把命题转为子句，否定目标，再推出矛盾。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | Robinson 将归结与合一结合起来，让自动证明器获得一种可系统实现的紧凑规则。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 它后来成为逻辑程序设计、SAT/SMT 谱系以及许多推理系统的基础。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Earlier theorem provers often needed many specialized inference rules. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Resolution reduced proof search to a small number of clause operations, making mechanized logic less ad hoc. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 早期定理证明器往往依赖许多专门推理规则。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 归结把证明搜索压缩为少量子句操作，让机械化逻辑不再那么临时拼装。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The key move is refutation: assume the claim is false, then repeatedly resolve complementary literals until the empty clause appears. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The key mechanism is Clause refutation with unification, which links the source material to the visible demo behavior. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键动作是反驳：先假设结论为假，再不断归结互补文字，直到推出空子句。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是带合一的子句反驳，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat resolution as a foundational proof method for symbolic AI and automated reasoning. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is visible in theorem proving, logic programming, SAT/SMT lineages, and constraint-based reasoning systems. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | proof/solved wording | 专家通常把归结法视为符号 AI 和自动推理的基础证明方法。 | needs-manual-source-review |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响体现在定理证明、逻辑程序设计、SAT/SMT 谱系和基于约束的推理系统中。 | structural-only |
| quote-work | en | no | no | A Machine-Oriented Logic Based on the Resolution Principle | structural-only |

| quote-work | zh | no | no | 基于归结原理的机器导向逻辑 | structural-only |

| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 互动演示会突出这些步骤如何把资料线索与可见的系统行为连接起来。 | structural-only |

| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the idea that stored examples and local similarity can be a model, not just training data. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把 KNN 视为基础性的非参数基线：简单、可解释，并且在距离有意义时表现很强。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于说明存储样本和局部相似性本身就可以构成模型，而不只是训练数据。 | structural-only |

### milestone-1970-shrdlu - SHRDLU

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| year-title | en | no | no | 1970: SHRDLU | structural-only |
| year-title | zh | no | no | 1970: SHRDLU | structural-only |
| location | en | no | no | MIT Artificial Intelligence Laboratory, Massachusetts, United States | structural-only |
| location | zh | no | no | 麻省理工学院 人工智能实验室，美国马萨诸塞州 | structural-only |

| description | en | no | no | SHRDLU showed that a computer could carry on a constrained but surprisingly rich dialogue about a toy blocks world. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Winograd combined parsing, planning, procedural semantics, and a small world model so natural-language commands could become robot-like actions. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Its power came from tight integration: language worked because the world was limited and explicitly represented. | structural-only |

| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 如果一个 NP 完全问题能被高效求解，那么 NP 中所有问题都能被高效求解。 | structural-only |

### milestone-1971-vc-theory - VC Theory

Sources:
- [On the Uniform Convergence of Relative Frequencies](https://epubs.siam.org/doi/10.1137/1116025) (Paper primary-candidate)

| description | en | no | no | VC theory explains why a model trained on limited examples can sometimes perform well on data it has never seen. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Vapnik and Chervonenkis connected learning, probability, and model capacity through measures such as VC dimension. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Their work became a foundation for statistical learning theory and shaped how machine learning thinks about generalization. | structural-only |

| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | The 1971 Vapnik-Chervonenkis paper made generalization a mathematical question about uniform convergence across a whole class of events or hypotheses. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Vapnik's 1995 book later synthesized the framework for statistical learning theory. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 瓦普尼克 和 切尔沃年基斯 1971 年论文把泛化变成了关于一整类事件或假设上一致收敛的数学问题。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 瓦普尼克 1995 年著作随后系统总结了统计学习理论框架。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The key display idea is the gap between fitting examples and performing on unseen data. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | VC dimension gives a way to reason about when model flexibility helps and when it becomes overfitting risk. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键展示点是“拟合样本”和“在未见数据上表现”之间的差距。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | VC 维提供了一种方法，用来理解模型灵活性何时有帮助、何时会带来过拟合风险。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat VC theory as one of the mathematical foundations of machine learning, while noting that classical bounds can be conservative for modern deep networks. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the language it gave researchers for model capacity, generalization, and learning from finite samples. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把 VC 理论视为机器学习的数学基础之一，同时也指出经典界对现代深度网络可能偏保守。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于为模型容量、泛化能力和有限样本学习提供了共同语言。 | structural-only |

### milestone-1974-frame - Frame

Sources:
- [A Framework for Representing Knowledge](https://courses.media.mit.edu/2004spring/mas966/Minsky%201974%20Framework%20for%20knowledge.pdf) (Paper primary-candidate)
- [Marvin Minsky obituary, MIT News](https://news.mit.edu/2016/marvin-minsky-obituary-0125) (Profile)

| Field | Locale | Risk | Manual Review | Claim | Status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| year-title | en | no | no | 1974: Frame | structural-only |
| year-title | zh | no | no | 1974: 框架 | structural-only |
| location | en | no | no | MIT Artificial Intelligence Laboratory, Massachusetts, United States | structural-only |
| location | zh | no | no | 麻省理工学院 人工智能实验室，美国马萨诸塞州 | structural-only |
| figure | en | no | no | Marvin Minsky - Author of the frame representation proposal | structural-only |
| figure | zh | no | no | 马文·明斯基 - 框架表示思想提出者 | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Frames proposed a way to represent stereotyped situations as structured bundles of slots, defaults, expectations, and procedures. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Instead of treating knowledge as isolated facts, frames organize what is normally true and what to check next. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | They influenced semantic networks, object-oriented knowledge systems, and the way AI systems model context. | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 框架提出了一种把典型情境表示为槽、默认值、预期和过程组合的方式。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 它不把知识看成孤立事实，而是组织“通常成立什么”和“接下来该检查什么”。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 它影响了语义网络、面向对象知识系统，以及 AI 系统建模上下文的方式。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Symbolic AI needed richer structures than flat predicate lists. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Frames offered reusable templates for scenes and concepts. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 符号 AI 需要比扁平谓词列表更丰富的结构。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 框架为场景和概念提供可复用模板。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | A frame stores slots such as parts, roles, defaults, and attached procedures; missing information can be filled by expectations. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The key mechanism is Structured slots with defaults and inheritance, which links the source material to the visible demo behavior. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 框架存储部件、角色、默认值和附加过程等槽；缺失信息可以由预期补齐。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是带默认值和继承的槽结构，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat frames as a central knowledge-representation idea from symbolic AI. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Their long-term legacy is the object-like organization of defaults, slots, and inheritance that influenced later knowledge bases, schemas, and semantic systems. | structural-only |

| description | en | no | no | Hopfield networks connected neural computation with physics. | structural-only |

| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Before deep learning, researchers were already asking how large sets of simple units could compute collectively. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Hopfield gave this question an energy-based formulation. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 在深度学习之前，研究者已经在追问大量简单单元如何集体计算。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | Hopfield 给这个问题提供了基于能量的表述。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The network updates units to reduce an energy function, so stored memories become stable attractors. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The key mechanism is Attractor dynamics and energy minimization, which links the source material to the visible demo behavior. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 网络更新单元以降低能量函数，因此被存储的记忆会成为稳定吸引子。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是吸引子动力学与能量最小化，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |

| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Their long-term legacy is the connection between memory, optimization, attractor dynamics, and statistical physics. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把 Hopfield 网络视为基于能量的神经计算史中的核心成果。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于连接了记忆、优化、吸引子动力学和统计物理。 | structural-only |

| description | en | no | no | Simulated annealing borrows from metallurgy: when temperature is high, the search can accept worse moves and explore; as temperature cools, it becomes more selective. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Kirkpatrick, Gelatt, and Vecchi showed how this idea could attack difficult optimization problems. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | The method became a classic bridge between physics, AI search, operations research, and combinatorial optimization. | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 模拟退火借鉴冶金过程：温度高时，搜索可以接受较差移动以扩大探索；温度降低后，它变得更挑剔。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 柯克帕特里克、Gelatt 和 Vecchi 展示了这一思想如何处理困难优化问题。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 该方法成为连接物理、AI 搜索、运筹学和组合优化的经典桥梁。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Many AI and engineering problems had enormous search spaces where greedy improvement got stuck. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Simulated annealing offered a principled way to make controlled uphill moves. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 许多 AI 与工程问题都有巨大搜索空间，贪心改进很容易卡住。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 模拟退火提供了一种有原则地进行受控“上坡”移动的方法。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | At high temperature, the algorithm explores boldly. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | As the system cools, it increasingly commits to lower-cost states, imitating the settling of physical materials. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 高温时，算法大胆探索；系统降温后，它越来越倾向低成本状态，模仿物理材料的稳定过程。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是带降温计划的概率搜索，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | proof/solved wording | Experts generally treat simulated annealing as a classic metaheuristic for escaping local optima, not as a guarantee of easy global optimization. | needs-manual-source-review |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the cooling metaphor for scheduling, routing, placement, and other hard combinatorial searches. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | proof/solved wording; superlative or benchmark wording | 专家通常把模拟退火视为用于跳出局部最优的经典元启发式方法，而不是轻松获得全局最优的保证。 | needs-manual-source-review |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于降温隐喻被用于调度、路径规划、布局和其他困难组合搜索。 | structural-only |

### milestone-1984-cart - CART

Sources:

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| year-title | en | no | no | 1984: CART | structural-only |
| year-title | zh | no | no | 1984: CART 决策树 | structural-only |
| location | en | no | no | University of California, Berkeley, Berkeley, United States | structural-only |
| location | zh | no | no | 加州大学伯克利分校，美国伯克利 | structural-only |

| figure | zh | no | no | 查尔斯·斯通 - CART 专著共同作者 | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | CART gave decision trees a durable statistical form: recursively split data, measure impurity, grow a tree, and prune it back to control overfitting. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | The method made models interpretable as if-then paths while still handling nonlinear interactions. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | It became a foundation for random forests, gradient boosting, and modern tree ensembles. | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | CART 为决策树提供了持久的统计形式：递归划分数据、度量不纯度、生成树，再通过剪枝控制过拟合。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 该方法让模型可以解释为 if-then 路径，同时能处理非线性交互。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 它成为随机森林、梯度提升和现代树集成方法的基础。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Decision rules were attractive because they were interpretable, but they needed a disciplined statistical procedure. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | CART supplied that procedure for both categorical and numeric outcomes. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 决策规则很有吸引力，因为它们可解释，但它们需要有纪律的统计过程。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | CART 为分类与数值输出都提供了这样的过程。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | CART grows a tree by choosing splits that make child nodes more homogeneous. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | It then prunes the tree so the final model balances fit and simplicity. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | CART 通过选择让子节点更同质的划分来生成树，再进行剪枝，使最终模型平衡拟合度与简洁性。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是递归划分与剪枝，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat CART as a foundational interpretable model and the basic unit behind stronger tree ensembles. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the split-and-prune logic used in explanation, tabular modeling, random forests, and gradient boosting. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把 CART 视为基础性的可解释模型，也是更强树集成方法背后的基本单元。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于划分与剪枝逻辑被用于解释、表格建模、随机森林和梯度提升。 | structural-only |
| quote-work | en | no | no | Classification and Regression Trees | structural-only |
| quote-authors | en | no | no | Leo Breiman, Jerome H. Friedman, Richard A. Olshen, and Charles J. Stone, Wadsworth / Routledge monograph, 1984 | structural-only |

### milestone-1988-td-update - Temporal-Difference Update

Sources:
- [Learning to Predict by the Methods of Temporal Differences](https://doi.org/10.1007/BF00115009) (Paper primary-candidate)
- [Richard Sutton homepage](http://incompleteideas.net/) (Homepage)
- [ACM 2024 Turing Award announcement](https://awards.acm.org/about/2024-turing) (Award primary-candidate)

| Field | Locale | Risk | Manual Review | Claim | Status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| year-title | en | no | no | 1988: Temporal-Difference Update | structural-only |
| year-title | zh | no | no | 1988: 时序差分更新 | structural-only |
| location | en | no | no | GTE Laboratories / University of Massachusetts lineage, United States and Canada | structural-only |
| location | zh | no | no | GTE 实验室 / 麻省大学学术谱系，美国与加拿大 | structural-only |
| figure | en | no | no | Richard Sutton - Author of temporal-difference learning | structural-only |
| figure | zh | no | no | 理查德·萨顿 - 时序差分学习提出者 | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Temporal-difference learning gave reinforcement learning a compact way to learn predictions from experience. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Instead of waiting for a final outcome, TD methods update value estimates using the next reward and the next prediction. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | This bootstrapping idea sits behind many later algorithms, including TD-Gammon, Q-learning, and actor-critic methods. | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 时序差分学习为强化学习提供了一种从经验中学习预测的紧凑方法。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | TD 方法不必等到最终结果，而是用下一步奖励和下一步预测来更新价值估计。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 这种自举思想支撑了 TD-Gammon、Q-learning 和 actor-critic 等后续算法。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Learning from delayed rewards required a way to assign credit before the entire episode ended. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | This context helps viewers place Temporal-Difference Update in the technical problems and research priorities of its time. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 从延迟奖励中学习需要一种在整个回合结束前分配信用的方法。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 这段背景帮助观众把时序差分更新放回当时的技术问题和研究重点中理解。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | TD compares the current prediction with a reward plus the next prediction, then nudges the current value toward that target. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The key mechanism is Bootstrapped value prediction, which links the source material to the visible demo behavior. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | TD 比较当前预测与“奖励加下一步预测”，再把当前价值向该目标推进。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是自举式价值预测，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat temporal-difference learning as a cornerstone of reinforcement learning. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the bootstrapping idea that value estimates can learn from later predictions, supporting Q-learning, actor-critic methods, and modern value-based control. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把时序差分学习视为强化学习的基石。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于提出价值估计可以从后续预测中自举学习，并支撑了 Q-learning、actor-critic 方法和现代基于价值的控制。 | structural-only |
| quote-work | en | no | no | Learning to predict by temporal differences | structural-only |
| quote-authors | en | no | no | Richard Sutton | structural-only |
| quote-work | zh | no | no | 通过时序差分学习预测 | structural-only |
| quote-authors | zh | no | no | 理查德·萨顿 | structural-only |

| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | Lasso 在回归中加入 L1 惩罚。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 该惩罚的几何形状自然产生精确零系数，因此预测与选择被绑定在一起。 | structural-only |

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| year-title | en | no | no | 2000: Spectral Clustering | structural-only |
| year-title | zh | no | no | 2000: 谱聚类 | structural-only |
| location | en | no | no | University of California, Berkeley, California, United States | structural-only |
| location | zh | no | no | 加州大学伯克利分校，美国加利福尼亚州 | structural-only |

| figure | zh | no | no | 吉滕德拉·马利克、吴恩达、亚伊尔·魏斯 - 谱聚类形式化的重要贡献者 | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Spectral clustering reframed grouping as a graph problem. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Points become nodes, similarities become weighted edges, and eigenvectors of graph matrices reveal low-dimensional structure where difficult cuts become easier to separate. | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 谱聚类把分组重新表述为图问题。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 样本成为节点，相似度成为带权边，图矩阵的特征向量揭示低维结构，使原本困难的切分更容易分离。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Image segmentation and data clustering needed methods that could separate non-convex groups without assuming spherical geometry. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | This context helps viewers place Spectral Clustering in the technical problems and research priorities of its time. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 图像分割与数据聚类需要能分离非凸群组的方法，而不假设簇是球形。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 这段背景帮助观众把谱聚类放回当时的技术问题和研究重点中理解。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The method builds an affinity graph, computes spectral embeddings from graph Laplacian eigenvectors, and clusters or cuts in that embedded space. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The key mechanism is Graph Laplacian eigenvector embedding, which links the source material to the visible demo behavior. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 该方法构建亲和图，从图拉普拉斯特征向量计算谱嵌入，再在嵌入空间中聚类或切分。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是图拉普拉斯特征向量嵌入，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat spectral clustering as a major graph-based approach to grouping non-convex data. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the use of graph Laplacian eigenvectors to connect image segmentation, manifold learning, graph clustering, and modern graph data analysis. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把谱聚类视为处理非凸数据分组的重要图方法。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于用图拉普拉斯特征向量连接图像分割、流形学习、图聚类和现代图数据分析。 | structural-only |
| quote-work | en | no | no | Normalized Cuts and Image Segmentation | structural-only |
| quote-authors | en | no | no | Jianbo Shi and Jitendra Malik | structural-only |
| quote-work | zh | no | no | 归一化切分与图像分割 | structural-only |
| quote-authors | zh | no | no | 史建波、吉滕德拉·马利克 | structural-only |

### milestone-2003-lda - Latent Dirichlet Allocation

Sources:
- [Latent Dirichlet Allocation](https://jmlr.org/papers/v3/blei03a.html) (Paper primary-candidate)
- [David M. Blei homepage](https://www.cs.columbia.edu/~blei/) (Author)
- [scikit-learn LatentDirichletAllocation](https://scikit-learn.org/stable/modules/generated/sklearn.decomposition.LatentDirichletAllocation.html) (Implementation)

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| year-title | en | no | no | 2003: Latent Dirichlet Allocation | structural-only |
| year-title | zh | no | no | 2003: 潜在狄利克雷分配 | structural-only |
| location | en | no | no | UC Berkeley / Stanford University, California, United States | structural-only |
| location | zh | no | no | 加州大学伯克利分校 / 斯坦福大学，美国加利福尼亚州 | structural-only |
| figure | en | yes | absolute-first-or-only wording; non-legacy risk claim | David Blei - First author of LDA | needs-manual-source-review |
| figure | zh | no | no | 戴维·布莱 - LDA 第一作者 | structural-only |
| figure | en | no | no | Michael Jordan - Co-author and probabilistic ML researcher | structural-only |
| figure | zh | no | no | 迈克尔·乔丹 - 共同作者，概率机器学习研究者 | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Latent Dirichlet Allocation gave topic modeling a clean probabilistic form. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Documents are mixtures of topics, topics are distributions over words, and inference estimates the hidden structure that produced observed text. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | LDA became a standard model for exploratory text analysis and probabilistic machine learning education. | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 潜在狄利克雷分配为主题模型提供了清晰的概率形式。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 文档是主题的混合，主题是词的分布，推断过程估计生成可见文本的隐藏结构。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | LDA 成为探索性文本分析和概率机器学习教学中的标准模型。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Text collections needed methods that discovered structure without hand-labeling every theme. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | LDA made the hidden-topic assumption explicit and probabilistic. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 文本集合需要无需手工标注每个主题就能发现结构的方法。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | LDA 把隐藏主题假设明确写成概率模型。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | Each document draws a topic mixture; each word chooses a topic and then a word from that topic’s distribution. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The key mechanism is Bayesian topic model with Dirichlet priors, which links the source material to the visible demo behavior. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 每篇文档抽取一个主题混合；每个词先选择主题，再从该主题词分布中生成词。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是带 Dirichlet 先验的贝叶斯主题模型，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat LDA as a classic probabilistic topic model and a teaching example for generative modeling. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is interpretability through latent structure, which remains useful even when neural embeddings and transformers perform better in many applications. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把 LDA 视为经典概率主题模型，也是讲解生成式建模的教学范例。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于通过潜在结构提供可解释性，即使神经嵌入和 Transformer 在许多应用中表现更好，这一点仍有价值。 | structural-only |
| quote-work | en | no | no | Latent Dirichlet Allocation | structural-only |
| quote-authors | en | no | no | David M. Blei, Andrew Y. Ng, Michael I. Jordan, Journal of Machine Learning Research, 2003 | structural-only |
| quote-work | zh | no | no | 潜在狄利克雷分配 | structural-only |

### milestone-2008-tsne - t-SNE

Sources:
- [Visualizing Data using t-SNE](https://jmlr.org/papers/v9/vandermaaten08a.html) (Paper primary-candidate)
- [Laurens van der Maaten homepage](https://lvdmaaten.github.io/) (Author page)
- [How to Use t-SNE Effectively, Distill](https://distill.pub/2016/misread-tsne/) (Guide)

| Field | Locale | Risk | Manual Review | Claim | Status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| year-title | en | no | no | 2008: t-SNE | structural-only |
| year-title | zh | no | no | 2008: t-SNE | structural-only |
| location | en | no | no | Tilburg University / University of Toronto, Netherlands and Canada | structural-only |
| location | zh | no | no | 蒂尔堡大学 / 多伦多大学，荷兰与加拿大 | structural-only |
| figure | en | no | no | Laurens van der Maaten - Co-author of t-SNE | structural-only |
| figure | zh | no | no | 劳伦斯·范德马滕 - t-SNE 共同作者 | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | t-SNE became one of the most recognizable tools for visualizing high-dimensional data. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | It converts pairwise neighborhood relationships into probabilities and then lays points out in a low-dimensional map with a heavy-tailed distribution. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | The result often reveals local clusters that are hard to see in raw feature space. | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | t-SNE 成为最具辨识度的高维数据可视化工具之一。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 它把成对邻域关系转为概率，再用重尾分布把点布置在低维图上。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 结果常能展示原始特征空间中难以看见的局部簇结构。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Researchers needed intuitive ways to inspect embeddings, digits, gene expression, and other high-dimensional data. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | This context helps viewers place t-SNE in the technical problems and research priorities of its time. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 研究者需要直观方法检查嵌入、数字、基因表达等高维数据。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 这段背景帮助观众把t-SNE放回当时的技术问题和研究重点中理解。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | t-SNE preserves local neighbor probabilities while using a t distribution to reduce crowding in the 2D map. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The key mechanism is Neighbor-preserving nonlinear embedding, which links the source material to the visible demo behavior. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | t-SNE 保持局部邻域概率，并用 t 分布减少二维图中的拥挤问题。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是保持邻域的非线性嵌入，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat t-SNE as a powerful exploratory visualization tool that must be interpreted carefully. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is making high-dimensional embeddings visually inspectable, while teaching users that cluster maps can be persuasive but not definitive evidence. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把 t-SNE 视为强大的探索性可视化工具，但也强调必须谨慎解读。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于让高维嵌入变得可视化可检查，同时提醒用户簇图有说服力但不是决定性证据。 | structural-only |

| quote-authors | en | no | no | Laurens van der Maaten | structural-only |
| quote-work | zh | no | no | 使用 t-SNE 可视化数据 | structural-only |

| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 经典强化学习有坚实理论，但从原始像素扩展到控制任务仍然困难。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | DQN 让这种扩展变得可见。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | Experience replay breaks correlations in recent experience, while a target network stabilizes value updates. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The key mechanism is Q-learning with convolutional networks, replay, and target networks, which links the source material to the visible demo behavior. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 经验回放打破近期经验的相关性，目标网络则稳定价值更新。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是结合卷积网络、经验回放与目标网络的 Q 学习，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat DQN as the breakthrough that made deep reinforcement learning visible and concrete. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the neural loop connecting perception, action, reward, replay, and value learning, despite ongoing sample-efficiency and stability challenges. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把 DQN 视为让深度强化学习变得可见且具体的突破。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于把感知、行动、奖励、经验回放和价值学习接成神经循环，尽管样本效率和稳定性问题仍存在。 | structural-only |

| description | en | no | no | Adam became one of the default optimizers of modern deep learning because it adapts each parameter step from running estimates of gradients and squared gradients. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Kingma and Ba published it in 2014 as a simple, efficient stochastic optimization method that worked well across noisy objectives. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Its influence is visible in nearly every deep-learning framework and in later variants such as AdamW. | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | Adam 之所以成为现代深度学习的默认优化器之一，是因为它用梯度与梯度平方的滑动估计来为每个参数自适应调整步长。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 金马 与 巴 在 2014 年提出这一简单、高效的随机优化方法，用来处理噪声目标函数。 | structural-only |

| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Researchers needed optimizers that reduced hand-tuning while still working with minibatches, sparse gradients, and nonstationary objectives. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 到 2014 年，深度网络越来越大，训练噪声也越来越明显。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 研究者需要一种减少手工调参、同时能处理小批量、稀疏梯度和非平稳目标的优化器。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | Adam merges the direction memory of momentum with the per-parameter scaling of RMSProp. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The result is a compact update rule that usually reaches useful training regimes quickly. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | Adam 把动量的方向记忆与 RMSProp 的逐参数缩放结合起来，形成紧凑的更新规则，通常能较快进入可用训练状态。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是一阶与二阶矩自适应更新，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat Adam as a practical default optimizer rather than a universal optimum. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is fast and stable neural-network training, plus a family of descendants such as AdamW and schedule-aware training recipes. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | superlative or benchmark wording | 专家通常把 Adam 视为实用默认优化器，而不是万能最优解。 | needs-manual-source-review |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于推动了快速、稳定的神经网络训练，并催生了 AdamW 和结合学习率计划的训练配方。 | structural-only |

### milestone-2014-dropout - Dropout

- [Improving neural networks by preventing co-adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/1207.0580) (Preprint primary-candidate)

| year-title | en | no | no | 2014: Dropout | structural-only |
| year-title | zh | no | no | 2014: Dropout | structural-only |
| location | en | no | no | University of Toronto, Toronto, Canada | structural-only |
| location | zh | no | no | 多伦多大学，加拿大多伦多 | structural-only |

| description | en | no | no | Dropout made overfitting less dangerous in large neural networks by randomly removing units during training. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Each minibatch effectively trains a thinned network, while test-time prediction approximates an ensemble. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | The idea became a standard regularizer across deep learning toolkits. | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | Dropout 通过在训练中随机移除神经元，让大型神经网络更不容易过拟合。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 每个小批量近似训练一个变薄的网络，测试时预测则近似集成。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 这个思想后来成为深度学习工具包里的标准正则化方法。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | As networks grew larger, memorization became a practical training problem. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Dropout offered a simple intervention that did not require changing the dataset. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 随着网络变大，记忆训练集成为实际问题。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | Dropout 提供了不必改变数据集的简单干预方式。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The core idea is to hide random units during training so hidden features cannot rely too strongly on each other. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The key mechanism is Randomly thinned networks for regularization, which links the source material to the visible demo behavior. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 核心思想是在训练时随机隐藏单元，使隐藏特征不能过度依赖彼此。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是随机变薄网络进行正则化，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat dropout as a simple and effective regularization idea whose value depends on architecture and scale. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the training-time noise principle, now taught alongside normalization, augmentation, and other regularizers. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把 Dropout 视为简单有效的正则化思想，但其价值取决于架构和规模。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于训练时引入噪声这一原则，如今常与归一化、数据增强和其他正则化方法一起讲解。 | structural-only |
| quote-work | en | no | no | Dropout: A Simple Way to Prevent Neural Networks from Overfitting | structural-only |
| quote-authors | en | no | no | Nitish Srivastava, Geoffrey Hinton, Alex Krizhevsky, Ilya Sutskever, Ruslan Salakhutdinov, JMLR, 2014 | structural-only |

| description | en | no | no | Earlier R-CNN systems depended on external region proposal algorithms, creating a bottleneck between feature extraction and detection. | structural-only |

| description | zh | no | no | 早期 R-CNN 系统依赖外部候选区域算法，在特征提取与检测之间形成瓶颈。 | structural-only |

| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | R-CNN 已经大幅提升目标检测精度，但外部候选区域生成让流水线变慢且不够统一。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 这段背景帮助观众把Faster R-CNN放回当时的技术问题和研究重点中理解。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | Faster R-CNN trains the network to propose boxes while it is already computing visual features. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | Detection becomes a learned pipeline rather than a hand-off between unrelated modules. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | Faster R-CNN 让网络在计算视觉特征的同时学习提出候选框。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 检测因此成为学习型流水线，而不是无关模块之间的交接。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat Faster R-CNN as a turning point that made object detection more end-to-end and learnable. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the proposal-and-recognition framework that still shapes how researchers explain accuracy, speed, and localization tradeoffs. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把 Faster R-CNN 视为让目标检测更端到端、更可学习的转折点。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于“候选区域 + 识别”框架仍塑造着研究者对精度、速度和定位权衡的解释。 | structural-only |

| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | AlexNet 和 VGG 之后，CNN 变得更深也更耗算力。 | structural-only |

| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | 1x1 bottlenecks keep this multi-branch design affordable. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | Inception 模块让网络同时使用多种感受野尺寸。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 1x1 瓶颈层让这种多分支设计在计算上可承受。 | structural-only |

| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the emphasis on parallel branches, bottlenecks, and explicit compute tradeoffs that influenced later block design and architecture search. | structural-only |

| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Rectified linear activation traces through early neural vision work and later became a standard activation for deep networks. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Its simple non-saturating shape helped train deeper models more effectively than many older squashing nonlinearities. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 整流线性激活可以追溯到早期神经视觉研究，后来成为深度网络的标准激活函数。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 它简单且不易饱和的形状，比许多早期压缩型非线性函数更有利于训练深层模型。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | Negative responses are clipped to zero while positive responses pass through linearly. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The interactive demo focuses on the steps that connect the source material to the visible system behavior. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 负响应被截断为零，正响应则线性通过。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 互动演示会突出这些步骤如何把资料线索与可见的系统行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat ReLU as a simple engineering choice whose impact was larger than its formula suggests. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the non-saturating activation pattern that helped deep networks train reliably and became a default component of modern architectures. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把 ReLU 视为一个简单工程选择，但它的影响远大于公式本身。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于非饱和激活模式帮助深层网络更可靠地训练，并成为现代架构的默认组件。 | structural-only |
| quote-work | en | no | no | Deep Sparse Rectifier Neural Networks | structural-only |

| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 兹米特里·巴赫达瑙、赵京贤和约书亚·本吉奥提出注意力机制，让神经翻译解码器能回看源句中的不同位置。 | structural-only |

| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | At each decoding step, attention scores source tokens and forms a context vector for the next translated word. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The model can therefore learn soft alignment instead of compressing the whole sentence into one fixed vector. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The interactive demo focuses on the steps that connect the source material to the visible system behavior. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 在每个解码步骤，注意力为源语言令牌打分，并形成用于生成下一个译词的上下文向量。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 因此模型可以学习软对齐，而不是把整句压缩成一个固定向量。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 互动演示会突出这些步骤如何把资料线索与可见的系统行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat neural attention for translation as the bridge from recurrent encoder-decoder systems to transformer-style architectures. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is making learned token-to-token relevance a central operation in language, vision, and multimodal AI. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把神经翻译中的注意力视为从循环编码器-解码器系统走向 Transformer 式架构的桥梁。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于让学习得到的令牌相关性成为语言、视觉和多模态 AI 的核心操作。 | structural-only |

| year-title | en | no | no | 2015: U-Net | structural-only |
| year-title | zh | no | no | 2015: U-Net | structural-only |
| location | en | no | no | University of Freiburg, Freiburg, Germany | structural-only |
| location | zh | no | no | 弗赖堡大学，德国弗赖堡 | structural-only |

| description | en | no | no | U-Net was designed for biomedical image segmentation, where labeled data can be scarce and boundary detail matters. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Its contracting path gathers context while the expanding path restores resolution, with skip connections carrying fine details across the U shape. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | The design escaped its original niche and became a general template for segmentation, restoration, diffusion models, and dense prediction. | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | U-Net 最初面向生物医学图像分割，在这类任务中标注数据稀缺且边界细节重要。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 收缩路径汇聚上下文，扩张路径恢复分辨率，跳跃连接则把精细信息跨过 U 形结构传递过去。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 这个设计后来走出原始领域，成为分割、图像复原、扩散模型和密集预测的通用模板。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Biomedical imaging needed models that could learn from limited annotations while preserving small structures. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Plain classification CNNs were not enough because the output had to align with every pixel. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 生物医学图像需要模型在有限标注下学习，并保留细小结构。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | 普通分类 CNN 不够，因为输出必须与每个像素对齐。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | U-Net pairs a context-gathering path with a resolution-restoring path. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | Skip connections reunite semantic context with local detail. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | U-Net 将收集上下文的路径与恢复分辨率的路径配对。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 跳跃连接把语义上下文与局部细节重新合在一起。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat U-Net as a canonical architecture for dense prediction and image restoration. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the encoder-decoder pattern with skip connections, which spread from biomedical segmentation to restoration, generative models, and diffusion backbones. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把 U-Net 视为密集预测和图像复原的经典架构。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于带跳跃连接的编码器-解码器模式，从生物医学分割扩展到图像复原、生成模型和扩散模型骨干网络。 | structural-only |
| quote-work | en | no | no | U-Net: Convolutional Networks for Biomedical Image Segmentation | structural-only |
| quote-authors | en | no | no | Olaf Ronneberger, Philipp Fischer, and Thomas Brox, Medical Image Computing and Computer-Assisted Intervention, 2015 | structural-only |
| quote-work | zh | no | no | U-Net：用于生物医学图像分割的卷积网络 | structural-only |

| description | en | no | no | YOLO reframed object detection as a single regression problem. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | Instead of proposing regions and classifying them separately, one network predicted bounding boxes and class probabilities from the whole image in one pass. | structural-only |
| description | en | no | no | The result made real-time object detection a mainstream engineering target. | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | YOLO 把目标检测重新表述为单次回归问题。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 它不再先提候选区域再逐个分类，而是让一个网络从整张图一次性预测边界框和类别概率。 | structural-only |
| description | zh | no | no | 这个思路让实时目标检测成为主流工程目标。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | Before YOLO, high-accuracy detectors often relied on multi-stage pipelines. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | en | no | no | YOLO asked what would happen if detection became one dense prediction problem. | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | YOLO 之前，高精度检测器常依赖多阶段管线。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Historical Background | zh | no | no | YOLO 追问：如果检测变成一个稠密预测问题会怎样？ | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The image is divided into a grid; each cell predicts boxes, confidence, and classes, all in one forward pass. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | en | no | no | The key mechanism is Single-shot grid-based object detection, which links the source material to the visible demo behavior. | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 图像被划成网格；每个网格单元一次前向传播就预测框、置信度和类别。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Core Idea | zh | no | no | 关键机制是基于网格的单阶段目标检测，它把资料线索与可见的演示行为连接起来。 | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | yes | no | Experts generally treat YOLO as the system that made real-time object detection a central benchmark goal. | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | en | no | no | Its long-term legacy is the framing of detection as fast single-pass prediction, influencing many later detector families and deployment expectations. | structural-only |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | yes | no | 专家通常把 YOLO 视为让实时目标检测成为核心基准目标的系统。 | low-priority-risk |
| commentary:Long-Term Legacy | zh | no | no | 它的长期影响在于把检测表述为快速的单次前向预测，并影响了许多后续检测器家族和部署预期。 | structural-only |
| quote-work | en | yes | no | You Only Look Once: Unified, Real-Time Object Detection | low-priority-risk |

### milestone-ai100-2017-densenet - DenseNet

Sources:
- [Densely Connected Convolutional Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/1608.06993) (Paper primary-candidate)
